<h3> ׳• - ׳›׳— ׳”׳¢׳•׳ ׳’ ׳›׳•׳׳ ׳‘׳×׳•׳›׳• ׳׳× ׳”׳©׳׳—׳” ׳•׳”׳‘׳›׳™ ׳‘׳‘׳× ׳׳—׳× </h3>
 ׳‘׳”׳׳›׳•׳× ׳©׳‘׳× ׳™׳©׳ ׳” ׳”׳׳›׳”, ׳©׳׳ ׳”׳‘׳›׳™ ׳¢׳•׳ ׳’ ׳׳•, ׳׳•׳×׳¨ ׳׳• ׳׳‘׳›׳•׳×. ׳‘׳™׳•''׳˜ ׳™׳©׳ ׳• ׳׳™׳¡׳•׳¨ ׳׳‘׳›׳•׳× ׳׳׳ ׳׳ ׳›׳ ׳–׳”׳• ׳‘׳›׳™ ׳©׳ ׳©׳׳—׳”, ׳’׳¢׳’׳•׳¢׳™׳, ׳‘׳›׳™ ׳“׳‘׳§׳•׳×, ׳׳©׳''׳› ׳‘׳©׳‘׳× ׳ ׳₪׳¡׳§ ׳‘׳©׳•''׳¢ ׳©׳׳•׳×׳¨ ׳׳‘׳›׳•׳× ׳‘׳›׳™ ׳©׳ ׳¢׳•׳ ׳’. ׳•׳׳׳• ׳“׳•׳§׳ ׳©׳׳—׳” ׳©׳ ׳“׳‘׳§׳•׳×, ׳׳׳ ׳’׳ ׳‘׳›׳™ ׳”׳׳•׳׳™׳“ ׳‘׳׳“׳ ׳¨׳•׳’׳¢ ׳•׳›׳“׳•', ׳׳•׳×׳¨ ׳׳‘׳›׳•׳×׳•, ׳›׳™ ׳¢׳•׳ ׳’ ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳• [׳•׳›׳™׳“׳•׳¢ ׳©׳”׳©׳‘׳× ׳”׳™׳ ׳¢׳•׳ ׳’, ׳•׳”׳™׳•''׳˜ - ׳©׳׳—׳”]. ׳›׳— ׳”׳¢׳•׳ ׳’ ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳•׳×׳• ׳›׳— ׳”׳›׳•׳׳ ׳‘׳§׳¨׳‘׳• ׳’׳ ׳׳× ׳”׳‘׳›׳™ ׳•׳’׳ ׳׳× ׳”׳©׳׳—׳” ׳‘׳‘׳× ׳׳—׳×. ׳©׳‘׳× ׳”׳•׳ ׳™׳•׳ ׳©׳׳—׳”, ׳•׳¢׳ ׳›׳ ׳–׳׳× ׳™׳© ׳‘׳• ׳׳§׳•׳ ׳׳‘׳›׳™ ׳©׳׳•׳׳™׳“ ׳¢׳•׳ ׳’. ׳™׳© ׳›׳׳ ׳׳× ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳”׳”׳×׳›׳׳׳•׳×, ׳©׳”׳©׳׳—׳” ׳•׳”׳‘׳›׳™ ׳׳×׳›׳׳׳™׳ ׳–׳” ׳‘׳–׳” ׳‘׳©׳‘׳×. ׳׳™׳ ׳ ׳₪׳¨׳“׳•׳×, ׳™׳©׳ ׳” ׳׳—׳“׳•׳× ׳׳—׳× ׳₪׳©׳•׳˜׳”, ''׳¨׳–׳ ׳“׳׳—׳“''. ׳”׳‘׳›׳™ ׳•׳”׳©׳׳—׳” ׳׳™׳ ׳ ׳©׳ ׳™ ׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳ ׳ ׳₪׳¨׳“׳™׳, ׳׳׳ ׳”׳›׳ ׳׳—׳“! ''׳›׳”׳“׳™׳ ׳§׳׳¦׳™׳ ׳“׳׳‘׳•׳©׳™׳ ׳׳™׳ ׳™׳” ׳•׳‘׳™׳”'', ׳”׳©׳׳—׳” ׳•׳”׳¢׳¦׳‘׳•׳×, ׳”׳¢׳¦׳‘׳™׳, ׳”׳¦׳׳¦׳•׳, ׳”׳’׳‘׳•׳ ׳•׳”׳‘׳׳×׳™ ׳‘׳¢׳ ׳’׳‘׳•׳ - ''׳¨׳–׳ ׳“׳׳—׳“''.

<h3> ׳™׳‘ - ׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳‘׳§׳‘''׳” ׳©׳™׳›׳•׳•׳ ׳• ׳׳”׳׳׳™׳ ׳‘׳¦׳“׳™׳§ ׳”׳׳׳™׳×׳™ </h3>
׳¢׳•׳׳§ ׳”׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳”׳™׳ ׳׳•׳×׳” ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳”, ׳©׳׳“׳ ׳׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳׳¦׳‘ ׳©׳׳™׳ ׳׳• ׳׳—׳™׳–׳” ׳‘׳›׳׳•׳, ׳•׳׳™׳ ׳׳• ׳×׳₪׳™׳¡׳” ׳‘׳›׳׳•׳, ׳׳™׳× ׳׳—׳©׳‘׳” ׳×׳₪׳™׳¡׳ ׳‘׳™׳”. ׳›׳׳©׳¨ ׳׳“׳ ׳׳ ׳×׳₪׳•׳¡ ׳‘׳›׳׳•׳, ׳‘׳׳₪׳©׳¨׳•׳×׳• ׳׳”׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳”׳×׳›׳׳׳•׳× ׳”׳׳׳™׳×׳™׳× ׳‘׳§׳‘''׳”. ׳›׳ ׳–׳׳ ׳©׳™׳© ׳׳• ׳׳™׳–׳•׳©׳”׳™ ׳׳—׳™׳–׳”, ׳׳£ ׳׳ ׳׳™׳ ׳” ׳‘׳‘׳•׳¨׳, ׳›׳™ ׳׳ ׳‘׳¦׳“׳™׳§ - ׳”׳¨׳™ ׳×׳₪׳•׳¡ ׳”׳•׳ ׳‘׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳©׳ ׳׳—׳™׳–׳”. ׳”׳§׳׳™׳₪׳” ׳©׳׳¢׳׳׳× ׳׳× ׳”׳’׳™׳׳•׳™ ׳”׳ ׳–׳›׳¨ ׳©׳ ׳”׳׳ ׳™׳“׳¢, ׳”׳™׳ ׳׳•׳×׳” ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳” ׳©׳׳“׳ ׳¢׳•׳©׳” ׳”׳‘׳“׳׳” ׳‘׳×׳•׳ ׳”׳¦׳“׳™׳§׳™׳ ׳¢׳¦׳׳. ׳›׳׳©׳¨ ׳™׳©׳ ׳” ׳”׳‘׳“׳׳” ׳‘׳×׳•׳ ׳”׳¦׳“׳™׳§׳™׳, ׳–׳•׳”׳™ ׳’׳•׳₪׳ ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳”׳©׳‘׳™׳¨׳” ׳׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳‘׳¦׳“׳™׳§׳™׳. ׳׳™׳ ׳¦׳ ׳©׳ ׳¡׳₪׳§ ׳©׳׳“׳ ׳‘׳“׳¢׳× ׳׳ ׳•׳©׳™׳× ׳׳ ׳™׳›׳•׳ ׳׳“׳¢׳× ׳׳™ ׳‘׳׳׳× ׳¦׳“׳™׳§ ׳•׳׳™ ׳׳, ׳׳‘׳ ׳”׳”׳‘׳“׳׳” ׳‘׳“׳¢׳× ׳׳•׳ ׳¢׳× ׳׳× ׳”׳¢׳׳׳× ׳”׳¦׳“׳™׳§ ׳׳”׳™׳“׳¢ ׳׳׳ ׳™׳“׳¢. ׳›׳׳ ׳ ׳¦׳¨׳›׳× ׳׳•׳×׳” ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳©׳׳“׳ ׳׳׳׳™׳ ׳‘׳§׳‘''׳” ׳©׳™׳×׳ ׳׳• ׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳•׳©׳׳׳•׳ ׳×׳• ׳‘׳¦׳“׳™׳§ ׳׳ ׳×׳”׳™׳” ׳₪׳’׳•׳׳”. ׳›׳™ ׳›׳ ׳–׳׳ ׳©׳׳“׳ ׳¨׳•׳¦׳” ׳׳‘׳¨׳¨ ׳׳× ׳”׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳¢''׳™ ׳“׳¢׳×, ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳ ׳¡׳” ׳׳‘׳¨׳¨: ׳–׳” ׳¦׳“׳™׳§, ׳–׳” ׳׳ ׳¦׳“׳™׳§ ׳•׳›׳•'. ׳ ׳׳¦׳, ׳©׳—׳–׳¨ ׳‘׳—׳–׳¨׳” ׳׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳”׳“׳¢׳×. ׳׳‘׳ ׳›׳׳©׳¨ ׳”׳׳“׳ ׳׳ ׳׳‘׳¨׳¨ ׳‘׳©׳›׳׳• ׳׳™ ׳¦׳“׳™׳§, ׳׳׳ ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳׳׳™׳ ׳‘׳§׳‘''׳” ׳©׳™׳›׳•׳•׳ ׳׳•׳×׳• ׳‘׳׳™ ׳׳”׳׳׳™׳ - ׳׳– ׳™׳© ׳›׳׳ ׳׳׳•׳ ׳” ׳©׳׳™׳׳” ׳׳—׳׳•׳˜׳™׳.
